				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/OIDplusPageAdminOIDInfoExport.class.php') !== '1b17c35d3e98e26f71a1e9255813b872e0028d51') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/OIDplusPageAdminOIDInfoExport.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 329\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 329') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
